[30;1m27 | [0m[35m<p>Markdown offers two styles of headers: <em>Setext</em> and <em>atx</em>.[0m
[30;1m28 | [0m[35mSetext-style headers for <code>&lt;h1&gt;</code> and <code>&lt;h2&gt;</code> are created by[0m
[30;1m29 | [0m[35m"underlining" with equal signs (<code>=</code>) and hyphens (<code>-</code>), respectively.[0m
[30;1m30 | [0m[35mTo create an atx-style header, you put 1-6 hash marks (<code>#</code>) at the[0m
[30;1m31 | [0m[35mbeginning of the line -- the number of hashes equals the resulting[0m
[30;1m32 | [0m[35mHTML header level.</p>[0m
[30;1m33 | [0m[35m<p>Blockquotes are indicated using email-style '<code>&gt;</code>' angle brackets.</p>[0m

[30;1m361 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m362 | [0m[35mDespite not being documented, previously an attribute list could be defined anywhere within a table [0m
[30;1m363 | [0m[35mapplied to the cell (`<td>` element). Now the attribute list must be defined at the end of the cell [0m
[30;1m364 | [0m[35mbe separated from the rest of the content by at least one space. This makes it easy to differentiate[0m
[30;1m365 | [0m[35mlists defined on inline elements within a cell and the attribute list for the cell itself. It is als[0m
[30;1m366 | [0m[35mwith how attribute lists are defined on other types of elements.[0m
[30;1m367 | [0m[35m[0m
